mxwwm014.dat

   ***********************************************************************************
   ** mxwwm014.dat:           Injector Backflow Example                             **
   ***********************************************************************************
   ***********************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                           **
   ** FILE:  MXWWM014.DAT  BASED ON MXSPR001.DAT                                                **
   **                                                                                           **
   ** MODEL: 13x14x6 GRIDS         4 OIL WELL SPACING               LAYERING SAND RESERVOIR     **
   **        SOLUTION GAS DRIVE    SOLVENT INJECTION                WELL WORKOVER               **
   **        GROUP VOIDAGE CONTROL                                                              **
   **        DEPLETION-WATERFLOOD FLOOD-PSEUDOMISCIBLE FLOOD                                    **
   **                                                                                           **
   ** USAGE: MODEL CROSS-FLOW THROUGH THE WELLBORE FOR A SOLVENT INJECTOR USING THE FULLY MIXED **
   **        ASSUMPTION                                                                         **
   **                                                                                           **
   ** IN MXSPR001.DAT, THE SOLVENT INJECTOR IS COMPLETED ONLY IN THE TOP LAYER. IN THIS EXAMPLE,**
   ** THE SOLVENT INJECTOR IS COMPLETED IN ALL SIX LAYERS.  DURING THE WATER INJECTION CYCLES,  **
   ** THE INJECTION RATE AT RESERVOIR CONDITIONS IS MUCH HIGHER THAN DURING THE SOLVENT         **
   ** INJECTION CYCLES.  THUS CROSS-FLOW OCCURS DURING THE SOLVENT INJECTION CYCLE AS PART OF   **
   ** A PRESSURE TRANSIENT.                                                                     **
   **                                                                                           **
   ***********************************************************************************************

mxwwm015.dat

   ***********************************************************************************
   ** mxwwm015.dat:            SETPI KEYWORD Example                                 *
   **                          and the use of the CMG Wellbore Calculator            *
   ***********************************************************************************
   ***********************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                           **
   ** FILE:  MXWWM015.DAT  BASED ON MXWWM014.DAT                                                **
   **                                                                                           **
   ** MODEL: 13x14x6 GRIDS         4 OIL WELL SPACING               LAYERING SAND RESERVOIR     **
   **        SOLUTION GAS DRIVE    SOLVENT INJECTION                WELL WORKOVER               **
   **        GROUP VOIDAGE CONTROL                                                              **
   **        DEPLETION-WATERFLOOD FLOOD-PSEUDOMISCIBLE FLOOD                                    **
   **        PERFORM MULTIPLE CHANGES IN WELL PI                                                **
   ** USAGE: SETPI KEYWORD TO EITHER REPRESENT A DECLINE IN THE WELL INDEX OR AN IMPROVEMENT.   **
   **        OR SPECIFY A USER DEFINED VALUE.                                                   **
   **        FOR THIS EXAMPLE, IT IS ASSUMED THAT ALL WELLS EXIBITS AN INITIAL DECLINE IN       **
   **        THEIR PRODUCTIVITY. 4 YEARS LATER A WORKOVER IS DONE TO RESTORE THE PRODUCTIVITYN  **
   **        TO ITS ORIGINAL VALUE. ONE YEAR LATER A FIELD MEASURED PRODUCTIVITY IS SPECIFIED.  **
   **        .........................                                                          **
   **   Assume that all well productivities has declined slightly.                              **
   **        *SETPI MULT   1     2     3     4    5        ** Multiply the current well         **
   **                    0.95  0.92   0.97  0.85  0.9      ** index by the specified value      **
   **                                                      ** for each well                     **
   **       *DATE 1996 12 31                                                                    **
   **       ..........................                                                          **
   **   Assume work over has been done to restore the previous damage.                          **
   **      *SETPI MULTO '*'              **MULTIPLY the Original WELLINDEX                      **
   **       1.0                          ** by a factor of 1.0                                  **
   **      *DATE 2000 12 31              ** the effect of SETPI start from now.                 **
   **       ...........................                                                         **
   **   Assume field test has yilded the following measurements .                               **
   **        *SETPI LIQ 1:3      **set the PI value based on the oil phase.                     **
   **         5.0 7.0 10.0      ** to 5,7 and 10.0 m3/day/kPa.                                  **
   **        *SETPI WAT 4:5     ** SETPI for wells  4 and 5(injectors.                          **
   **         6.00              ** to 6.                                                        **
   **        *DATE 2001 01 31                                                                   **
   **                                                                                           **
   **        THE CMG WELLBORE CALCULATOR WAS USED TO GENERATES THE WELLBORE TABLES USED UNDER   **
   **        THE PTUBE KEYWORD.                                                                 **
   **                                                                                           **
   ***********************************************************************************************

mxwwm030.dat

   ****************************************************************************
   ** wmwwm030.dat:  Production Manifold with Minimum Pressure Constraint    **
   ****************************************************************************
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** FILE:   wmwwm030.dat                                                             **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** MODEL:  9x5x3 GRID.          TWO GATHERING CENTRE MODEL WITH GAS INJECTION.      **
   **         PRODUCTION MANIFOLDS.   MINIMUM MANIFOLD PRESSURE GROUP CONSTRAINT.      **
   **         PRESSURE TRANSLATION OF GROUP PRESSURE TARGETS.                          **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** This is a 9x5x3 cartesian grid gas injection problem with two gathering centres. **
   ** One gathering centre has a minimum production manifold pressure specified;       **
   ** the group enforces this pressure as the target once the constraint has been      **
   ** violated.  The other production group has no pressure constraint defined.        **
   ** Gas injection is under voidage replacement group control.                        **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   ** CONTACT:    CMG,   (403)531-1300;   282-6495 (fax);support@cmgl.ca    (Internet) **
   **************************************************************************************

mxwwm033.dat

   ******************************************************************************
   ** wmwwm033.dat:  VFPINJ table and VFPPROD table with ALQ                   **
   ******************************************************************************
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** FILE:   wmwwm033.dat                                                             **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** MODEL:  9x5x3 GRID.   TWO PRODUCTION MANIFOLDS. ONE GAS INJECTION MANIFOLD.      **
   **  PRODUCTION MANIFOLDS ON COMPRESSOR PRESSURE TARGET.                             **
   **  INJECTION MANIFOLD WITH BOTH RATE AND COMPRESSOR PRESSURE MAXIMUM.              **
   **  VFPPROD/VFPINJ TABLES TO DEFINE PRESSURE DROP BETWEEN SURFACE AND MANIFOLD.     **

   **  MORE THAN ONE ALQ VALUE FOR PRODUCTION.                                         **
   **                                                                                  **

   **                                                                                  **
   ** This is a 9x5x3 cartesian grid gas injection problem with two production         **
   ** manifold gathering  centres and one gas injection manifold gathering centre.     **
   ** The two production manifolds have a target compressor (surface) pressure         **
   ** specified.  The gas injection manifold has maximum rate and surface pressure     **
   ** constraints specified; these are enforced as targets when violated. The          **
   ** pressure drops from manifold to surface are computed from VFPPROD and VFPINJ     **
   ** tables;  the VFPPROD tables include rows corresponding to different value of the **
   ** ALQ.                                                                             **

   ******************************************************************************
   ** mxwwm034.dat:  Well before type, inactive layer status, and WLISTSHUT    **
   ******************************************************************************
   ***********************************************************************************
   **                                                                               **
   ** FILE:   mxwwm034.dat                                                          **
   **                                                                               **
   ** MODEL:  9x5x3 GRID.                                    WLISTSHUT-WLISTOPEN    **
   **         WELLS NAMED, PERF'D, TYPED AT DIFFERENT TIMES                         **

   **                                                                               **
   **                                                                               **
   ***********************************************************************************
   **                                                                               **
   **  This template illustrates three features :                                   **
   **  (1) Wells may be named at one time, have perforations defined later,         **
   **      and still later have type and constraints defined and begin operation.   **
   **  (2) The WLISTSHUT and WLISTOPEN keywords which allow a list of wells to be   **
   **      shut and later reopened without disturbing the initial pattern of shut   **
   **      and AUTODRILL wells.                                                     **
   **  (3) Inactive well layers (those not listed on the most recent PERF line)     **
   **      have their status written to RESULTS as CLOSED and is so displayed.      **
   **                                                                               **
   **                                                                               **
   ***********************************************************************************

mxwwm037.dat

   ******************************************************************************
   ** mxwwm037.dat: Group Target Apportionment with PRIORITY ranking           **
   ******************************************************************************
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** FILE:   MXWWM037.DAT                                                             **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** MODEL:  38x40x8   PRIMARY PRODUCTION IN A RESERVOIR WITH EDGE AQUIFER            **
   ** APPOR-METHOD KEYWORD   PRIOR-FORM KEYWORD                                        **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** This data set illustrates the use of the following apportionment methods         **
   ** through keyword *APPOR-METHOD to meet multi-level group targets:                 **
   **     (1) Instantaneous Potential (*IP)                                            **
   **     (2) Guide Rates (*GUIDE)                                                     **
   **         Supply guide rates by *GUIDEP (production) and/or GUIDEI (injection)     **
   **     (3) Internal Guide Rates (*INGUIDE)                                          **
   **     (4) Priority Ranking (*PRIOR)                                                **
   **         Supply priority formula by *PRIOR-FORM                                   **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** The priority ranking apportionment makes it possible to, for example, obtain     **
   ** as low a GOR as possible when producing oil at a specified group rate by         **
   ** assigning as much production as possible to the wells with the lowest GORs.      **
   **                                                                                  **
   **                                                           based on mxwwm010.dat  **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** Jan 2007 Modified to not use the WHP constraint                                  **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   ** CONTACT:    CMG,   (403)531-1300;   282-6495 (fax);support@cmgl.ca    (Internet) **
   **************************************************************************************

mxwwm038.dat

   ******************************************************************************
   ** mxwwm038.dat:  Fluid Redistribution via Modelshut Wells                  **
   ******************************************************************************
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** FILE:   mxwwm038.dat                                                             **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** MODEL:  21x1x15       CROSS-FLOW THROUGH MODELSHUT WELLS                         **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** This is a vertical cross-section problem consisting of two disconnected          **
   ** reservoirs with two wells, Connect-p and Connect-i, the only means of            **
   ** communication between the different reservoirs. Persistent backflow occurs.      **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** Initially the two regions are in vertical flow equilibrium. The deepest          **
   ** reservoir receives injected water from the main water injector (well 4);         **
   ** the two connecting wells (well 2, 3) are completed in both of the regions.       **
   ** The shallowest reservoir produces through well 1 with a constant bottom-hole     **
   ** pressure. There is no production directly from the deepest region.  Fluid flows  **
   ** from the deepest region through the wellbores of well 2 and 3 to the shallowest  **
   ** one, and then to the surface through the producing well 1.                       **
   ** Symmetric solutions are expected.                                                **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** Three types of drawdown constraints (DWN/DWA/DWB) are tested.                    **
   **        DWN -- drawdown at reference layer                                        **
   **              (disallowed when perforated in null/pinched block)                  **
   **        DWA -- maximum drawdown in all open layers                                **
   **        DWB -- PI-weighted average drawdown                                       **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   ** CONTACT:    CMG,   (403)531-1300;   282-6495 (fax);support@cmgl.ca    (Internet) **
   **************************************************************************************

mxwwm039.dat

   ******************************************************************************
   ** mxwwm039.dat:         Drawdown Constraint DWA and DWB Test               **
   ******************************************************************************
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** FILE:   mxwwm039.DAT                                                             **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** MODEL:  10x1x15       Drawdown Constraint DWA and DWB Test                       **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** Coats, K.H., Thomas, L.K., and Pierson, "Compositional and Black Oil Reservoir   **
   ** Simulation", 13th SPE Symposium on Reservoir Simulation, 1995 (SPE 29111).       **
   ** This is a vertical cross-section problem consisting of three communicating       **
   ** with one well, Producer 2, the only means of communication between the different **
   ** reservoirs. Severe backflow occurs. Tests for Well 2 to run on:                  **
   **    (1) Low STO rate, and/or                                                      **
   **    (2) Low DWB (PI-weighted average drawdown), or                                **
   **    (3) MODELSHUT (Shutin above formation)                                        **
   **                                                   based on mxwwm013.dat          **
   **************************************************************************************
   ** CONTACT:    CMG,   (403)531-1300;   282-6495 (fax);support@cmgl.ca    (Internet) **
   **************************************************************************************

mxwwm047.dat

   ******************************************************************************
   ** mxwwm047.dat:            Well management: gas lift optimization          **
   ******************************************************************************
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** FILE:   MXWWM047.DAT                                                             **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** MODEL:  20x20x2   PRIMARY PRODUCTION BY GAS LIFTING USING A PTUBE1 TABLE         **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** This example illustrates the use of the *GLIFT *OPT keywords followed by well's  **
   ** name list or numbers. The wells' gas lift injection rates are calculated         **
   ** automatically according to the specifications listed under the *GLOPT keyword.   **
   ** It demonstrates the use of the PTUBE1 table. Results should be identical to      **
   ** mxwwm008.dat                                                                     **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************

   **  PRODUCTION MANIFOLDS ON COMPRESSOR PRESSURE TARGET.                             **

   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** This is a 9x5x3 cartesian grid gas injection problem with two production         **
   ** manifold gathering centres and one gas injection manifold gathering centre.      **
   ** The two production manifolds have a target compressor (surface) pressure         **
   ** specified.  The gas injection manifold has maximum rate and surface pressure     **
   ** constraints specified; these are enforced as targets when violated. The          **
   ** pressure drops from manifold to surface are computed from PTUBE1 and ITUBE1      **
   ** tables;  the PTUBE1 tables include rows corresponding to different value of the  **
   ** ALQ. This data set should produce results identical to mxwwm033.dat              **

mxwwm054.dat

   ******************************************************************************
   ** mxwwm054.dat:         Well management:    ON-TIME option with layer lump **
   ******************************************************************************
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** FILE:             MXWWM054.DAT                                                   **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** MODEL:  25x65x2   PRIMARY PRODUCTION IN A RESERVOIR WITH GAS CAP                 **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** This example illustrates the use of the layer lumping option and in particular   **
   ** the LAYERLUMP_ACTR keyword.                                                      **
   ** The default case for the layer lumping option is to write out instanteneous      **
   ** rates as opposed to actual or on time values. If ON-TIME factors other than unity**
   ** are specified, as is the case in this dataset, then the keyword LAYERLUMP_ACTR is**
   ** required to write out on time or actual rates. All well rate values written out  **
   ** to the RESULTS plotting program are on time or actual rates. In this dataset the **
   ** use of the *LAYERLUMP_ACTR keyword ensures that the oil rate for well 8, 'PRD06' **
   ** matches the rate for layer lump 'lump1' which has its members the two layers     **
   ** specified for well 8. To verify plot oil rate SC for well 8 and the oil rate for **
   ** 'lump1' available in special history. If the *LAYERLUMP_ACTR keyword is          **
   ** is commented out then the oil rate plotted from the well record will not match   **
   ** the oil rate for 'lump1' from special history. This is because the values from   **
   ** well record are actual or on time averaged rates and for the lump they will be   **
   ** instanteneous numbers. This dataset is a modified version of mxwwm011.dat        **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   ** CONTACT:    CMG,   (403)531-1300;   282-6495 (fax);support@cmgl.ca    (Internet) **
   **************************************************************************************

   **   Keywords Tested                                                                **
   **                                                                                  **
   **    *GCONCYCLE_START 'WFGROUP1'                                                   **
   **       *cycstreams 'WATI' 'SOLI'                                                  **
   **       *nparts 2                                                                  **
   **       *ncycles 20                                                                **
   **       *targettypes                                                               **
   **          'WATI' 'STW' 'STW'                                                      **
   **          'SOLI' 'STS' 'STS'                                                      **
   **       *maxrates                                                                  **
   **          **'WATI' -0.5 -0.5                                                      **
   **          'SOLI' 0.   1000.                                                       **
   **       *vrepfr                                                                    **
   **          'WATI' 2.0 0.0                                                          **
   **          **'SOLI' -0.5 -0.5                                                      **
   **       *maxcums                                                                   **
   **          'WATI' 56000.0  1.0                                                     **
   **          'SOLI'  1.0     83000.0                                                 **
   **       *maxbhp                                                                    **
   **          'WATI' 27000.0  1.0                                                     **
   **          'SOLI'  1.0     27000.0                                                 **

   **       *dtwcyc 0.01 0.01                                                          **

   **                                                                                  **

   **       *SHUTIN 4 5                                                                **
   ** ** Trigger1 condition will be satisfied at a later time than trigger2            **
   ** ** at least 60 days, STO running at 50                                           **
   **       *TRIGGER 'trigger1' *ON_WELL 'OIL1' STO-RP < 55 *AVRGTIME 60.0             **
   **          *TARGET *STL 'OIL1'                                                     **
   **              30.0                                                                **
   **     *END_TRIGGER                                                                 **
   ** ** Trigger2 satisfied as soon as group cycling ends since                        **
   ** ** sto wells 'oil1', 'oil2', 'oil3' = 50, 39, 0 respectively, < 55               **
   **       *TRIGGER 'trigger2' *ON_WELL 'OIL*' STO-RP < 55                            **
   **          *TARGET *STL '@'                                                        **
   **              35.0                                                                **
   **       *END_TRIGGER                                                               **
   **  *END_TRIGGER                                                                    **

mxgmc004.dat

   *****************************************************************************
   ** Template (mxgmc004.dat):  2D RADIAL GRID                                **
   *****************************************************************************
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** FILE :  MXGMC004.DAT                                                             **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** MODEL:  SINGLE WELL                                      FIELD UNITS             **
   **                                                          13X1X4 RADIAL GRID      **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** USAGE:  ILLUSTRATES THE COUPLED GEOMECHANICAL OPTION IN IMEX                     **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** Purposes:                                                                        **
   **               Different rock types are assigned in the geomechanics              **
   **               section due to different Young's modulus on each layer.            **
   **               Output stresses, subsidence and displacement vector.               **
   **               *RIGIDTOP keyword is applied so that the cap of reservoir          **
   **               is not allowed moving upward.                                      **
   **               The value of Young's modulus is obtained from the formula given by **
   **               Settari and Mourits (SPEJ, pp. 219-226,1998)                       **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   ** CONTACT:    CMG,   (403)531-1300;   282-6495 (fax);support@cmgl.ca    (Internet) **
   **************************************************************************************

mxgmc006.dat

   *****************************************************************************
   ** Template (mxgmc006.dat):  3D CARTESIAN GRID                             **
   *****************************************************************************
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** FILE :  MXGMC006.DAT                                                             **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** MODEL:  SINGLE WELL (OVERBURDEN LOADS)                   FIELD UNITS             **
   **         ELASTIC MODEL                                    11X11X3 CARTESIAN GRID  **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** USAGE:  ILLUSTRATES THE COUPLED GEOMECHANICAL OPTION IN IMEX                     **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** Purposes:                                                                        **
   **   This example has some new features in the geomechanics section                 **
   **   as follows:                                                                    **
   **   @ Overburden loads are represented by distributed load on the                  **
   **     cap of the reservoir (*DLOADBC).                                             **
   **   @ Body force of the reservoir is expressed through the combination             **
   **     of two keywords : *GLOADBC and SPECGRAV                                      **
   **   @ Using keyword *PLSTRAINY : plane strain computed along J direction           **
   **     ie. the direction is perpendicular to the plane. It is also noted            **
   **     that since the keyword *PLSTRAINY is used, the distributed loads             **
   **     must be entered in the clockwise direction.                                  **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   ** CONTACT:    CMG,   (403)531-1300;   282-6495 (fax);support@cmgl.ca    (Internet) **
   **************************************************************************************

mxgmc007.dat

   *****************************************************************************
   ** Template (mxgmc007.dat):  3D CARTESIAN GRID                             **
   *****************************************************************************
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** FILE :  MXGMC007.DAT                                                             **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** MODEL:  SINGLE WELL                                        SI UNIT               **
   **         ELASTIC MODEL                                      5x3x4 CARTESIAN GRID  **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** USAGE:  ILLUSTRATES THE COUPLED GEOMECHANICAL OPTION IN IMEX                     **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** Purposes:                                                                        **
   **    The new keyword *GEODOMAIN is introduced in the geomechanics section.         **
   **    Only sub regions defined by the keyword *GEODOMAIN are computed by            **
   **    the geomechanics module. Outside the regions, emperical models of             **
   **    porosity implemented in the reservoir simulator (if applicable)               **
   **    are applied.                                                                  **
   **                                                                                  **
   **    *SOLVERG *AIMSOL  :  Applied AIMSOL in the geomechanics module.               **
   **                                                                                  **
   **    *NOCOUPERM:  Disables all the deformation-dependent permeability data, which  **
   **                 is keyword *GPERMLC added before and after *NOCOUPERM.  The      **
   **                 result is the same as having no GPERMLC data.                    **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   ** CONTACT:    CMG,   (403)531-1300;   282-6495 (fax);support@cmgl.ca    (Internet) **
   **************************************************************************************

   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** FILE :  MXGMC015_OB.DAT                                                          **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** MODEL:  SINGLE WELL                                      FIELD UNITS             **
   **         ELASTIC MODEL                                    5X5X2 CARTESIAN GRID    **

   ** USAGE:  ILLUSTRATES *OUTBOARD *REPLAY FEATURE FOR MXGMC015 DEFORMATIONS          **
   **                                                                                  **
   **  Illustrate and verify the use of *OUTBOARD to provide geomechanical deformation **
   **  generated by outboard software.  For the case provided here, these deformations **
   **  were generated by IMEX case "mxgmc015.dat" and written to the *OUTBOARD record  **
   **  file via command-line argument "-obrec_geomech":                                **
   **                                                                                  **
   **     imex -f mxgmc015.dat -obrec_geomech                                          **
   **                                                                                  **
   **  This file is a copy of "mxgmc015.dat" with all the geomechanics data removed.   **
   **  Instead, this data uses *OUTBOARD in *REPLAY mode to read *UPOR_CP and          **
   **  *UPOR_REF obtained from case MXGMC015, for each grid block and at each time     **
   **  step.  The results are physically the same to MXGMC015 results.                 **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   ** CONTACT:    CMG,   (403)531-1300;   282-6495 (fax);support@cmgl.ca    (Internet) **
   **************************************************************************************

mxgmc038.dat

   *****************************************************************************
   ** Template (mxgmc038.dat):  2D RADIAL GRID                                **
   *****************************************************************************
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** FILE :  MXGMC038.DAT                                                             **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** MODEL:  SINGLE WELL                                      FIELD UNITS             **
   **         Mohr-Coulomb model                               31X1X2 RADIAL GRID      **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** USAGE:  ILLUSTRATES THE COUPLED GEOMECHANICAL OPTION IN IMEX                     **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** Purposes:                                                                        **
   **        Demonstrate how stresses repond in an infinite Mohr-Coulomb medium when   **
   **        a hole is suddently removed.                                              **
   **        Demonstrate how the dilation angle is used in Mohr-Coulomb model.         **
   **        To see the difference in results, the dilation angle can be changed       **
   **        within the range 0 and friction angle.                                    **
   **        If the dilation angle and friction angle are not the same, the plastic    **
   **        flow rule is nonassociated. Otherwise, the rule is considered as an       **
   **        associated one.                                                           **
   **        Uses keyword NINCS to divide a large load into a number of small even     **
   **        loads to avoid unstability.                                               **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   ** CONTACT:    CMG,   (403)531-1300;   282-6495 (fax);support@cmgl.ca    (Internet) **
   **************************************************************************************

mxgmc039.dat

   *****************************************************************************
   ** Template (mxgmc039.dat):  3D CARTESIAN GRID                             **
   *****************************************************************************
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** FILE :  MXGMC039.DAT                                                             **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** MODEL:  SINGLE WELLS                                     SI UNITS                **
   **         Linear elastic model                             10X10X1 CARTESIAN GRID  **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** Purposes:                                                                        **
   **        Illustrate how the Skempton's effect to an undrained condition            **
   **        Illustrate Mandel-Cryer's effect to a drained condition                   **
   **        Skempton's effect can only be observed when a sudden load is applied to a **
   **        surface of reservoir. This load will cause changes in pore pressure       **
   **        and in porosity. Compressive load causes an increase in pore pressure     **
   **        and tensile load cause a decrease in pore pressure.                       **
   **        Mandel-Cryer's effect is a phenomenon of pore pressure increasing higher  **
   **        than its initial value after the Skempton's effect when the fluid is      **
   **        withdrawn.                                                                **
   **        Besides, in order to solve such a problem, GCOUPLING 3 and number of      **
   **        coupling iterations are used.                                             **
   **        The number of coupling iterations (NCOUPLING) can be any large positive   **
   **        interger. The convergence of coupling is controlled by the tolerance      **
   **        given in the data; for instance, STRESSTOL.                               **
   **        Output total normal stresses (TSTRESI TSTRESJ TSTRESK)                    **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   ** CONTACT:    CMG,   (403)531-1300;   282-6495 (fax);support@cmgl.ca    (Internet) **
   **************************************************************************************

mxgmc047.dat

   *****************************************************************************
   ** Template (mxgmc047.dat):  3D CARTESIAN GRID                             **
   *****************************************************************************
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** FILE :  MXGMC047.DAT                                                             **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** MODEL:  SINGLE WELL                                      FIELD UNITS             **
   **         Linear elastic model                             31X30X2 3D RADIAL GRID  **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** USAGE: Unload stress                                                             **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** Purposes:                                                                        **
   **        Demonstrate how stresses repond in an infinite Mohr-Coulomb medium when   **
   **        a hole is suddently removed.                                              **
   **        Demonstrate how the dilation angle is used in Mohr-Coulomb model.         **
   **        To see the difference in results, the dilation angle can be changed       **
   **        within the range 0 and friction angle.                                    **
   **        If the dilation angle and friction angle are not the same, the plastic    **
   **        flow rule is nonassociated. Otherwise, the rule is considered as an       **
   **        associated one.                                                           **
   **        Uses keyword NINCS to divide a large load into a number of small even     **
   **        loads to avoid unstability.                                               **
   **        This test case is for 3D radial grid. Its results can be compared         **
   **        with those of test case stgeo038.dat for 2D radial grid.                  **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   ** CONTACT:    CMG,   (403)531-1300;   282-6495 (fax);support@cmgl.ca    (Internet) **
   **************************************************************************************

mxgmc055.dat

   *****************************************************************************
   ** Template (mxgmc055.dat):  3D CARTESIAN GRID                             **
   *****************************************************************************
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** FILE :  MXGMC055.DAT                                                             **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** MODEL:  SINGLE WELL                                      FIELD UNITS             **
   **         RESERVOIR REGION                                 11X11X10 CARTESIAN GRID **
   **         GEOMECHANICS REGION                              48x48x26 CARTESIAN GRID **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** USAGE:  ILLUSTRATES THE COUPLED GEOMECHANICAL OPTION IN IMEX                     **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** Purposes:                                                                        **
   **   The purpose of this problem is to demostrate how the dual grids are used.      **
   **   Features:                                                                      **
   **     Translation is applied to geomechanical grids so that reservoir region is    **
   **       located at the middle of the entire field.                                 **
   **     The reservoir region is soft whereas its surrounding rock is hard.           **
   **     There is no flow calculation in the surrounding region of the reservoir.     **
   **     Local refined grids are used in the reservoir.                               **
   **                                                                                  **
   **   This problem is based on the problem 1 in SPE 79709 by Dean et al.             **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   ** CONTACT:    CMG,   (403)531-1300;   282-6495 (fax);support@cmgl.ca    (Internet) **
   **************************************************************************************

mxgmc058.dat

   *****************************************************************************
   ** Template (mxgmc058.dat):  2D CARTESIAN GRID                             **
   *****************************************************************************
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** FILE :  MXGMC058.DAT                                                             **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** MODEL:  SINGLE WELL                                      SI UNITS                **
   **         Modified Cam Clay (MCC) model                    1X13X7 CARTESIAN GRID   **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** USAGE:  Distributed loads on 2D element edges                                    **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** Purposes:                                                                        **
   **        Illustrate how the Skempton's effect to an undrained condition            **
   **        Skempton's effect can only be observed when a sudden load is applied to a **
   **        surface of reservoir. This load will cause changes in pore pressure       **
   **        and in porosity. Compressive load causes an increase in pore pressure     **
   **        and tensile load cause a decrease in pore pressure.                       **
   **                                                                                  **
   **        Besides, in order to solve such a problem, GCOUPLING 3 and number of      **
   **        coupling iterations are used.                                             **
   **        The number of coupling iterations (NCOUPLING) can be any large positive   **
   **        interger. The convergence of coupling is controlled by the tolerance      **
   **        given in the data; for instance, STRESSTOL.                               **
   **        Output total normal stresses (TSTRESI TSTRESJ TSTRESK), first and second  **
   **        invariant stress tensor (STRESINVF STRESINVS), void ratio (VOIDRATIO).    **
   **        Modified Cam Clay (MCC) constitutive model is used in this simualtion.    **
   **        Some data of the model were taken from the reference                      **
   **        (Comp. Methods. Appl.Mech. Engrg., Vol 155, pp. 73-95, 1998)              **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   ** CONTACT:    CMG,   (403)531-1300;   282-6495 (fax);support@cmgl.ca    (Internet) **
   **************************************************************************************

mxgmc060.dat

   *****************************************************************************

   **       Applied dual grids, refined grid and pseudo dilation model                 **
   **                                                                                  **

mxgmc090.dat

   *****************************************************************************
   ** Template (mxgmc090.dat):  Pre Fracture Model                            **
   *****************************************************************************
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** FILE :  MXGMC090.DAT                                                             **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** MODEL:  TWO WELLS                                        FIELD UNITS             **
   **         Barton-Bandis Dual Porosity Model                25X1X25 CARTESIAN GRID  **
   **         2D FRACTURE NETWORK                                                      **
   **         CAPILLARY PRESSURES AFFECT MATRIX-FRACTURE TRANSFER                      **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** USAGE:  ISOTHERMAL DUAL PERM MODEL WITH CAPILLARY PRESSURE EFFECTS               **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** Purposes:                                                                        **
   **       In this test problem,  a pre fracture is demonstrated.                     **
   **       At the beginning time, the fracture exists but its width is zero.          **
   **       Therefore, there is no permeability affected by geomechanics.              **
   **       At the later time, when fluid enters the fracture, the width increases     **
   **       and leads to higher fracture permeability. Within the pre fracture         **
   **       length, there is no need a fracture criterion since the fracture           **
   **       was already created.                                                       **
   **       The reservoir is fractured in all directions and the                       **
   **       dual perm model is used to simulate the reservoir behavior.                **
   **                                                                                  **
   **       Gas-oil and oil-water capillary pressures in both the matrix and           **
   **       fracture affect matrix-fracture transfer term.                             **
   **                                                                                  **
   **       Based on mxgmc060.dat                                                      **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   ** CONTACT:    CMG,   (403)531-1300;   282-6495 (fax);support@cmgl.ca    (Internet) **

mxgmc093.dat

   *****************************************************************************
   ** Template (mxgmc093.dat):  3D CARTESIAN GRID                             **
   *****************************************************************************
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** FILE :  MXGMC093.DAT                                                             **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** MODEL:  TWO WELLS                                    FIELD UNITS                 **
   **         Barton-Bandis Dual Permeability Model        100X100X1 CARTESIAN GRID    **
   **         3D FRACTURE NETWORK WITH SHEAR FRACTURING                                **
   **         CAPILLARY PRESSURES AFFECT MATRIX-FRACTURE TRANSFER                      **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** USAGE:  ILLUSTRATES THE COUPLED GEOMECHANICAL OPTION IN IMEX                     **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** Purposes:                                                                        **
   **    Shear fracturing and Barton-Bandis models are applied to a dual permeability  **
   **    model for fracture closure. The reservoir is fractured in all directions and  **
   **    the Dual Perm model is used to simulate the reservoir behaviour.              **
   **                                                                                  **
   **    A parent well is a producer which gererates shear fractures in a region of    **
   **    withdrawn fluid and higher compressive stresses.                              **
   **    A child or infill well is an injector located parallel to the parent well.    **
   **    When a child well is opened, the increase in pressure in the region around    **
   **    it reduces the effective stress so that the fracture due to tensile stress    **
   **    may happen. The fluid from the injectors will travel to the parent well and   **
   **    affect to the production (based on mxgmc060).                                 **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   ** CONTACT:    CMG,   (403)531-1300;   282-6495 (fax);support@cmgl.ca    (Internet) **
   **************************************************************************************

mxgmc094.dat

   *****************************************************************************
   ** Template (mxgmc094.dat):  3D CARTESIAN GRID                             **
   *****************************************************************************
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** FILE :  MXGMC094.DAT (based on mxgmc088)                                         **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** MODEL:  SINGLE HORIZONTAL WELL                           FIELD UNITS             **
   **         STAGE FRACTURES, ELASTIC MODEL                                           **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** USAGE:  ILLUSTRATES THE COUPLED GEOMECHANICAL OPTION IN IMEX                     **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** Purposes:                                                                        **
   **     In this test problem, hydraulic fracturing model is applied to a dual        **
   **     perm model. Fractures will initiate and propagate in 3D.                     **
   **     Fracture permeability is computed based on the fracture width which is       **
   **     calculated from the split nodes between elements.                            **
   **     In order to create the fracture, the horizontal well is opened at            **
   **     different stages. Fracture opening and closure are controlled by             **
   **     *GBCPFACT and *GBCUFACT. Pressure used for geomechanics is controlled        **
   **     by *GPSCALING.                                                               **
   **     If GPSCALING = 0; gemoechanics will use the fracture pressure in reservoir   **
   **     If GPSCALING = 1; gemoechanics will use the matrix pressure in reservoir     **
   **     If 0 < GPSCALING < 1; geomechanics will use pressure scaled by the factor    **
   **                                                                                  **
   **     Reservoir grids: 31 30 50   - Cartesian grid                                 **
   **     Geogrids       : 31 34 50   - Cartesian grid                                 **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   ** CONTACT:    CMG,   (403)531-1300;   282-6495 (fax);support@cmgl.ca    (Internet) **
   **************************************************************************************

mxgmc095.dat

   *****************************************************************************
   ** Template (mxgmc095.dat):  3D CARTESIAN GRID                             **
   *****************************************************************************
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** FILE :  MXGMC095.DAT                                                             **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** MODEL:  TWO WELLS                                    FIELD UNITS                 **
   **         Barton-Bandis Dual Permeability Model        100X100X1 CARTESIAN GRID    **
   **         3D FRACTURE NETWORK WITH SHEAR FRACTURING                                **
   **         CAPILLARY PRESSURES AFFECT MATRIX-FRACTURE TRANSFER                      **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** USAGE:  ILLUSTRATES THE COUPLED GEOMECHANICAL OPTION IN IMEX                     **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** Purposes:                                                                        **
   **    Shear fracturing and Barton-Bandis models are applied to a dual permeability  **
   **    model for fracture closure. The reservoir is fractured in all directions and  **
   **    the Dual Perm model is used to simulate the reservoir behaviour.              **
   **                                                                                  **
   **    A parent well is a producer which gererates shear fractures in a region of    **
   **    withdrawn fluid and higher compressive stresses.                              **
   **    A child or infill well is an injector located parallel to the parent well.    **
   **    When a child well is opened, the increase in pressure in the region around    **
   **    it reduces the effective stress so that the fracture due to tensile stress    **
   **    may happen. The fluid from the injectors will travel to the parent well and   **
   **    affect to the production (based on mxgmc060 and mxgmc093).                    **
   **    In this example, permeability changed due to shear fracturing and total       **
   **    tensile stress are used.                                                      **

mxgmc100.dat

   *****************************************************************************
   ** Template (mxgmc100.dat):  3D CARTESIAN GRID                             **
   *****************************************************************************
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** FILE :  MXGMC100.DAT                                                             **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** MODEL:  NO WELL                                          SI UNITS                **
   **         Linear Elastic Model                             5x15x10 CARTESIAN GRID  **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** Purposes:                                                                        **
   **        Illustrate how the Skempton's effect to an undrained condition            **
   **        Skempton's effect can only be observed when a sudden load is applied to a **
   **        surface of reservoir. This load will cause changes in pore pressure       **
   **        and in porosity. Compressive load causes an increase in pore pressure     **
   **        and tensile load cause a decrease in pore pressure.                       **
   **        Mandel-Cryer's effect is a phenomenon of pore pressure increasing higher  **
   **        than its initial value after the Skempton's effect when the fluid is      **
   **        withdrawn.                                                                **
   **        Besides, in order to solve such a problem, *GCOUPLING 3 and number of     **
   **        coupling iterations are used.                                             **
   **        The number of coupling iterations (*NCOUPLING) can be any large positive  **
   **        interger. The convergence of coupling is controlled by the tolerance      **
   **        given in the data; for instance, *GPTOLMUL.                               **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   ** CONTACT:    CMG,   (403)531-1300;   282-6495 (fax);support@cmgl.ca    (Internet) **
   **************************************************************************************

   **                                                                                  **
   ** MODEL:  21x21x1 Grid                                                             **

mxtrc021.dat

   ******************************************************************************
   ** mxtrc021.dat:            Tracers though Cross-Flowing Wells              **
   ******************************************************************************
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** FILE:   mxtrc021.dat                                                             **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** MODEL:  21x1x15        TRACERS IN CROSS-FLOWING WELLS                            **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   **                                                                                  **
   ** This is a vertical cross-section problem consisting of two disconnected          **
   ** reservoirs with two wells, Connect-p (MODELSHUT) and Connect-i, the only means   **
   ** of communication between the different reservoirs. Persistent backflow occurs.   **
   **                                                                                  **
   ** Two water injection tracers are assigned respectively for the main injector and  **
   ** the secondary one. The main tracer starts to show up in the upper reservoir via  **
   ** both of the communicating wells, while the secondary tracer cannot reach the     **
   ** lower reservoir. Exam tracers in the main producer for water allocation.         **
   **                                                                                  **
   **************************************************************************************
   ** CONTACT:    CMG,   (403)531-1300;   282-6495 (fax);support@cmgl.ca    (Internet) **
   **************************************************************************************
